					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Amber &amp; Muse - Your wedding blog</h2>				</div>

				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
									<p>Getting married in the vineyards? Saying &#8220;I do&#8221; right on the coast? Or perhaps a romantic castle with medieval charm? There are at least as many ideas as there are weddings. The Real Weddings are dedicated to the perfect day in the most beautiful locations in the world. From the Alpine chalet to the Tuscan country house to the exotic fairy tale, you will write enchanting chapters of your magical love.</p><p>PHOTOGENE IDEAS<br>No more &#8220;wedding dress is a wedding dress&#8221;: The beauty of the moment is of course also expressed in the dress, gown, train and suit. Unique photo shoots play with the wedding theme in a variety of ways. Artful inspiration, magical color schemes and clever decorating ideas cleverly think outside the box with a knack for perfect style.</p><p>A TOAST TO YOUNG LOVE<br>Can you still remember how it all started? Young love overcomes boundaries and makes the impossible possible. Celebrate the breathtakingly beautiful moments before the wedding with engagement parties, engagements in the most romantic places in the world and episodes of lingering and pausing. Couple shots create lasting memories as a diary of your love.</p><p>STYLE AND BEAUTY<br>Every wedding should have its own unmistakable, unique style. In addition to the matching, highly individual decorations, which underline the theme in a variety of ways and emphasize it in all its facets, the bride often takes center stage.</p><p>Fashion and beauty are central anchor points of the upcoming festivities. How about simple understatement? Or would you prefer extravagance and luxury? Beauty is in the eye of the beholder, and you know exactly whose eye it is.</p><p>BE INSPIRED!<br>Sometimes the planning can be overwhelming. So many possibilities, so many details &#8211; it&#8217;s easy to get lost. Discover the many different faces of love with the large wedding guide inspiration world. A variety of possible combinations unite the romantic with the rustic, bring pure luxury to the beach or show what is actually possible with the popular color white.</p><p>HONEYMOON<br>It&#8217;s not just the wedding itself that creates unforgettable memories, the honeymoon in particular crowns the young couple&#8217;s happiness in many different ways. What does your perfect honeymoon look like? Perhaps you appreciate the idyllic and secluded, would like to exercise in the great outdoors or simply lounge on the beaches of the world&#8217;s most beautiful wellness oases? There are no limits to your ideas.</p><p>Of course you will find many more ideas for the wedding of your dreams. In the wedding guide you will find comprehensive tips on the right vendors, style ideas and many more exciting shots. One thing is already certain: your celebration of love will be as individual, flashy or understated as you are.</p>								</div>
